They prominently advertise their vegetarian and vegan offerings...yet a phone call placed to management reveals there is fish stock and chicken broth in EVERYTHING, even those things marked vegan! What the...?!

I'm sorry, please remind me what kind of plants chickens and fish grow on?

This is unacceptable, and their "oh well" attitude about it, once confronted, is unconscionable.

They are dosing unwitting vegetarians and vegans with the very ingedients they are dining there to avoid. That's just laziness at best, and outright sinister at worst.

VEGANS AND VEGETARIANS, BOYCOTT THIS PLACE!!!

There are plenty of other options where you won't be exposed to animal ingedients, and where the integrity of your choices and commitment is properly respected.</Text><Pics>None< /Pics>< Resp>

First let me state that the food is okay. However, their pricing is ridiculous. We ordered spicy noodles with 1/2 shrimp and 1/2 chicken. The cost of the spicy noodles with just shrimp is $12.95. We paid $14.95 (since we added chicken) and there were 2 shrimp in the entire dish along with some grossly overcooked chicken. I also ordered panaang curry with 1/2 tofu and 1/2 vegetables. I think there were 4 pieces of tofu. If you stick to the menu with one item you will probably be okay. For me....I won't be back.</Text>

<user_name>Cynthia De Gutierrez< /user_name>< review>
The location was really good because one can do other things while in that area, like do grocery shopping at Cardenas, or go to Pep Boys for little  things for the car, or check out the Verizon store .

The office space is well-designed with private areas for checking in for appointments and airing your concerns to the customer representative; the waiting area has good seating capacity with soft comfortable chairs and  a view to a wide screen TV; there was also quite  a good selection of frames to choose from.

The examination rooms were secured and private and had the up-to-date vision-testing paraphernalia.

I was really impressed with the Optometrist, Dr. Shin. He exuded confidence that he knew exactly what he was doing and he was calm and very professional yet friendly as he explained the condition of my eyes and the course of action I need to take to preserve them or to prevent further damage to my beginning cataract. I would definitely recommend him to my family and friends. He did not rush and he answered  all my questions kindly and with efficiency.
On the medical side of this clinic, I would give it a "10"

BUT on the sales side- I found a great disparity between the "special $99.00 deal of the day" and the "custom eyeglasses" which are costly.
It is not only the physical location of the frames that relegated them to having red tags, but the attitude that the sales personnel exhibited as I was transferred to view these cheaper alternatives. I feel that it is a fantastic thing for the Clinic to offer these bargains and I would have felt privileged to have purchased from that stock. I really just wanted a spare glasses,  My experience in choosing between what  I wanted but did not want to afford and the $99 specials could have been more satisfying if the person serving my needs had given that cheaper choice the same importance as the more expensive ones.  As it was, I felt that I should just go somewhere else to get my glasses; a place where there can be mutual satisfaction in whatever package I choose to purchase. I hope that this review will be taken in the spirit it was given. Vision Express Optometry has so much going for them already, this " glitch", I'm sure, can easily be "tweaked" :) Good luck !</review>

She was told its 1st come 1st serve basis. So we showed up right when doors opened walked in and saw 3 tables with "reserved" signs on  them. We asked the bartender how we could get tables or even reserve them. We told her what we were told. Her reply is "I literally have no idea. That comes from the owner".  We thought that was weird but settled for bar sitting even though we knew it wasn't going to be enough space for us all. As time went on now 3hrs into the show  I wanted to try some of my friends mimosa. So I poured 2 oz in my 4 oz water cup. With quickness the male bartender jumped down my throat. Going off on me about how I didn't pay for the mimosa. And I told him no my friend did I just wanted to try it. He continued to tell me I couldn't bc I didn't pay for it.
